         <h1 class="article_title" itemprop="headline name">
          50 Hottest NFL Fans
         </h1>
         <h4 class="article_author" itemprop="author">
          <address class="article_author-info" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
           By
           <a class="article_author-link" href="/users/456335-zack-pumerantz" itemprop="url" title="Zack Pumerantz">
            <span itemprop="name">
             Zack  Pumerantz
            </span>
           </a>
           ,
           <span class="author-rank">
            Analyst
           </span>
          </address>
          <time class="article_timestamp" data-updated_at="1318864573" itemprop="datePublished">
           Oct 17, 2011
          </time>
         </h4>

            <img alt="50 Hottest NFL Fans" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/620/Giants-4_crop_262x400.jpg?1318864982" width="262"/>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While teams around the
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/nfl">
             NFL
            </a>
            continue to fight for league-wide respect and appreciation, their fans are battling to prove their worth to the camera and competing fanbases.
           </p>
           <p>
            It's a long season that is tedious in preparation, and only some of the many fans can handle the tough task at hand.
           </p>
           <p>
            Many will attempt to attract an audience and impress the camera, but only few can reach the upper echelon of beauty.
           </p>
           <p>
            With the timing of this list, some stats may have changed and several teams' records adjusted, but it's the aesthetic pleasure that matters most. Thanks guyism for the photos.
           </p>
           <p>
            Here are the 50 hottest fans in the NFL. Thanks
            <a href="http://guyism.com/topics/hot-nfl-fans" target="_blank">
             Guyism
            </a>
            for most of the photos.
           </p>
           <p>
            Enjoy.
           </p>
          </div>

         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             50. Skeptical Optimism
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:223px">
            <img alt="50. Skeptical Optimism" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/623/4265705953_6bb53069fd_crop_223x420.jpg?1318864992" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="223"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This smile will quickly turn into a frown if Josh Freeman's Bucs can't find their winning ways.
           </p>
           <p>
            After a mediocre 48-3 showing against the 49ers, Tampa Bay is looking to show its legitimacy and prove all the doubters wrong.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Bucs' fans already have.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-3 cf display-none " data-page="3">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             49. Appreciating the Past
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:315px">
            <img alt="49. Appreciating the Past" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/624/4266452084_46d1d2752b_crop_315x420.jpg?1318864996" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="315"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After a 4-1 start to the season for the San Diego Chargers, they now face a bye week, giving them time to appreciate the throng of beautiful fanatics who sport their bright jerseys.
           </p>
           <p>
            It's curious as to whether these fans know that
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/ladainian-tomlinson">
             LaDainian Tomlinson
            </a>
            is now wearing green and white in New York.
           </p>
           <p>
            Either way, we're impressed.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-4 cf display-none " data-page="4">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             48. The Reason for Their False Starts
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:315px">
            <img alt="48. The Reason for Their False Starts" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/621/603066_crop_315x420.jpg?1318865001" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="315"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After the Chicago Bears' offensive line was flagged for nine false starts in their 24-13 loss to the Detroit Lions, fans were baffled and frustrated.
           </p>
           <p>
            It seems likely that their beautiful fans made the trip from the Windy City to see their team in action, unaware that Da Bears couldn't handle the distractions.
           </p>
           <p>
            Seemingly hard to focus when these fans grace the stands.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-5 cf display-none " data-page="5">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             47. Out with the Old, in with the New
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:203px">
            <img alt="47. Out with the Old, in with the New" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/625/4266452772_d087ce7740_crop_203x420.jpg?1318865005" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="203"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Fans in Green Bay can't possibly be surprised by the team's undefeated start.
           </p>
           <p>
            It's clear from this confident pose that the Cheeseheads expect another title, and require domination to please them.
           </p>
           <p>
            Perhaps she'll want to multiply that jersey number by three.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             46. Remembering the Good Times
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:301px">
            <img alt="46. Remembering the Good Times" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/626/4266452892_fcca6d1cec_crop_301x420.jpg?1318865006" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="301"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This fan is seemingly reminiscing about the good times, when the Vikings prospered.
           </p>
           <p>
            Chester Taylor spent four years in Minnesota, and ran for 1,216 yards and six touchdowns in his final season on the team.
           </p>
           <p>
            Fans don't forget.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-7 cf display-none " data-page="7">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             45. A Case of Gang Green
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:315px">
            <img alt="45. A Case of Gang Green" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/627/4266453202_85f62e45fd_crop_315x420.jpg?1318864972" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="315"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Fans are seemingly on the edge of their seats in preparation for Monday's matchup between the struggling Jets and the hapless 'Fins.
           </p>
           <p>
            With seven consecutive losses dating back to last season, Miami is yearning for any speck of promise.
           </p>
           <p>
            If Gang Green relinquishes this game to Matt Moore and the depleted Dolphins, they might as well throw in the towel for the rest of the season.
           </p>
           <p>
            Former Jets Gameday Host Jenn Sterger will undoubtedly be clinging to her jersey for 60 minutes.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             44. Fight for Your Right
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:280px">
            <img alt="44. Fight for Your Right" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/628/american_football_girl_11_nicefun.net_63_crop_280x420.jpg?1318864972" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="280"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While most fans sit back and judge their team one snap at a time, this beauty takes matters into her own hands.
           </p>
           <p>
            Whether she is an actual fan or a hopeful rookie is unclear. However, she can clearly intimidate her opponent.
           </p>
           <p>
            It's working.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             43. False Sense of Pride
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:180px">
            <img alt="43. False Sense of Pride" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/629/Bears-2_display_image_crop_180x400.jpg?1318864976" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="180"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            She can't possibly be smiling about last week's debacle against the hungry Lions.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, running back
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/matt-forte">
             Matt Forte
            </a>
            's 205 yards on the ground against Carolina and 116 against Detroit gives Bears fans hope that winning is on the horizon.
           </p>
           <p>
            But with 18 sacks on the season,
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/jay-cutler">
             Jay Cutler
            </a>
            may find himself on a stretcher before the team can turn their season around.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             42. Dark and Ominous
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:199px">
            <img alt="42. Dark and Ominous " data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/630/Bengals-2_display_image_crop_199x400.jpg?1318864976" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="199"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This threatening, albeit sexy pose is seemingly a metaphor for the future in Cincinnati.
           </p>
           <p>
            The fiery pack of Bengals have displayed heart and the zealous determination to win at any cost thus far this season.
           </p>
           <p>
            All their wins have come through fourth-quarter comebacks.
           </p>
           <p>
            They've come a long way
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/articles/890638-the-boston-red-sox-and-the-most-dysfunctional-teams-in-sports-history/page/21" target="_blank">
             since 2006
            </a>
            .
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             41. At a Crossroads
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:293px">
            <img alt="41. At a Crossroads" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/669/Panthers-3_crop_293x387.jpg?1318865005" height="387" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="293"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Like her favorite team, this fan feels cornered.
           </p>
           <p>
            Despite the stellar play of rookie No. 1 overall pick Cam Newton, the youthful Carolina Panthers can't seem to secure a victory.
           </p>
           <p>
            In time, their improved offense and inspired defense will hope to please their beleaguered fans.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             40. Cruising Along
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:321px">
            <img alt="40. Cruising Along" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/631/Bills-2_display_image_crop_321x400.jpg?1318864972" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="321"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            It was easy for fans to lay back and relax when their beloved Bills were one inexcusable second-half collapse against the Bengals away from a perfect record.
           </p>
           <p>
            With wins against the disappointing Eagles and the potent Patriots, Buffalo was showing their worth to the rest of the league.
           </p>
           <p>
            Whether they can continue to flourish is debatable.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             39. Praying to the NFL Gods
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:266px">
            <img alt="39. Praying to the NFL Gods " data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/632/Broncos-1_display_image_crop_266x400.jpg?1318864972" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="266"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Fans' call for
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/tim-tebow">
             Tim Tebow
            </a>
            seems to have
            <a href="http://espn.go.com/nfl/story/_/id/7087660/tim-tebow-replaces-kyle-orton-denver-broncos-starting-quarterback-john-fox-says">
             finally been answered by John Fox
            </a>
            , with the former Gator ready to grab hold of the reins.
           </p>
           <p>
            With the team currently sitting at 1-4, the former Heisman Trophy winner won't need to do much to impress.
           </p>
           <p>
            This beauty is hoping that her John Elway Jersey can sway the fortunes of this hyped prospect.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>

            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/ben-roethlisberger">
             Ben Roethlisberger
            </a>
            seems to play better when hurt, following his five touchdown passes against a promising Titans despite a sprained left foot.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, Pittsburgh is clearly yearning for the bullish-type rusher that can exhaust opposing defenses like Jerome Bettis used to.
           </p>
           <p>
            This fan would be a perfect change-of-pace back for Rashard Mendenhall.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             34. An Unavoidable Distraction
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:280px">

An Unavoidable Distraction" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/638/hot_nfl_jersey_5_crop_280x420.jpg?1318864991" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="280"/>

            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/eli-manning">

            </a>
            , with his talent and intelligence, continues to make bone-headed mistakes in crucial moments since winning the miraculous 2007 Super Bowl.
           </p>
           <p>
            These fans always seem to pop into his mind at the wrong time.
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             33. The Three Musketeers
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:277px">
            <img alt="33. The Three Musketeers" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/639/hot-football-girls_crop_277x420.jpg?1318864997" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="277"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While most fans have clear dedications to specific teams and honorable loyalties to several players, these beauties seemingly prance about searching for only the best.
           </p>
           <p>
            They may not travel to every stadium, yearning for prosperity, but they sure do shine in front of cameras with their love of football.
           </p>
           <p>
            Teams are always working hard to gain their allegiance.
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             32. An Opportune Time
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:269px">

           </p>
           <p>
            This one is quite excited for the opportunity.
           </p>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             31. Sweeter Than a Graham Cracker
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:280px">
            <img alt="31. Sweeter Than a Graham Cracker" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/640/Hot-Girls-NFL-Jerseys-5_crop_280x420.jpg?1318864999" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="280"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Not only have the Saints gone three games in a row without fumbling for the first time since 2008 before Sunday's games, but they now have an effective new weapon in Tight End Jimmy Graham.
           </p>
           <p>
            With over 100 yards receiving in the same three-game stretch, Graham is quickly garnering plenty of fan appreciation.
           </p>
           <p>
            This is all the motivation he needs.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             30. Waiting to Take off
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:500px">
            <img alt="30. Waiting to Take off" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/641/HotJetsGirlLeonWashingtonjersey_crop_500x333.jpg?1318865005" height="333" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="500"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Jets fans seemingly miss 5'8" bulldozer Leon Washington since he took his talents to Seattle last year.
           </p>
           <p>
            While he only has 39 yards on the ground, his returning ability separates him from the rest of the pack.
           </p>
           <p>
            These vintage jerseys continue to excite.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             29. Unstoppable Support
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:600px">
            <img alt="29. Unstoppable Support" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/642/hottest-nfl-fan-151_crop_600x374.jpg?1318864972" height="374" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="600"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            A bye week couldn't have come at a better time for the Cowboys last week, following their destructive second-half performance against the Lions, specifically
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/tony-romo">
             Tony Romo
            </a>
            's three costly interceptions.
           </p>
           <p>
            Fan support, however, never dwindled.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             28. Draft Day Surprises
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:480px">
            <img alt="28. Draft Day Surprises" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/643/image006_crop_480x420.jpg?1318864972" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="480"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This is a site not often seen in New York, yet it creates a subtle warmth and camaraderie between two struggling fanbases.
           </p>
           <p>
            Both fans left the 75th NFL Draft pleased with their team's selections.
           </p>
           <p>
            2010 Giants first-rounder (No. 15 overall) Jason Pierre-Paul is currently third in the league in sacks with 6.5 and Jets former first-rounder (No. 29 overall) Kyle Wilson is finally feeling comfortable in his nickel cornerback role with 11 tackles.
           </p>
           <p>
            Both teams were pleased with the fan support.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             27. Long Hair, Don't Care
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:266px">
            <img alt="27. Long Hair, Don't Care" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/644/Jags-2_display_image_crop_266x400.jpg?1318864974" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="266"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            When the Blaine Gabbert era in Jacksonville began in Week 2, fans were excited for the future, albeit worried about rookie mistakes.
           </p>
           <p>
            With a completion percentage of 49.5, Gabbert will have to stop glaring at his fans during plays and start reading defenses.
           </p>
           <p>
            We understand it's hard to stay focused.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             26. Misa Campo Charges Ahead
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:279px">
            <img alt="26. Misa Campo Charges Ahead" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/645/misacampo_crop_279x420.jpg?1318864977" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="279"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Canadian model Misa Campo has no problem engaging audiences and exciting the camera on any given shoot.
           </p>
           <p>
            It seems as if she's trying to attract a different kind of audience... a louder, more fanatical one.
           </p>
           <p>
            Her obvious allegiance to the San Diego Chargers is duly noted, and her slight smile is a result of their 4-1 record.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             25. Diamond in the Rough
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:266px">
            <img alt="25. Diamond in the Rough" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/647/nfl-girl-jerseys_crop_266x372.jpg?1318864978" height="372" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="266"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With seven touchdowns and a 92.9 quarterback rating, most fans in Dallas would expect their statistically sound signal caller to be flawless in crunch time.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, superfluous mistakes have led his Cowboys to a mundane 2-3 record.
           </p>
           <p>
            Perhaps their future lies in the beautiful crowd.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             24. The Good Old Days
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:336px">
            <img alt="24. The Good Old Days" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/648/nfl-jersey-girls-36_crop_336x420.jpg?1318864979" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="336"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While he may be in New York now, LaDainian Tomlinson still has a loyal throng of followers in San Diego.
           </p>
           <p>
            Once known as arguably the most prolific running back in the league, Tomlinson is surely missing his days as a cut-back monster who couldn't be contained.
           </p>
           <p>
            Fans clearly miss him as well.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             23. Tough Skinned
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:349px">
            <img alt="23. Tough Skinned" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/650/nflgirl5_crop_349x400.jpg?1318864990" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="349"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Many may be naturally baffled by the recent success of the Washington Redskins, but it's easy to why they're tougher and better groomed for a weekly battle in the trenches.
           </p>
           <p>
            If this sexy fan is giving us any insight into the training regimen of this team, it's clear that they practice in uncomfortable weathers.
           </p>
           <p>
            It may be a form of resistance training... unless these fans are present.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             22. Steeler Swagger
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:281px">
            <img alt="22. Steeler Swagger" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/661/SteelersGirl_crop_281x420.jpg?1318864994" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="281"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With six Super Bowl wins, the Steelers are quite the accomplished teams, and their fans know it.
           </p>
           <p>
            While we're intimidated by her calmness in front of a Ninja Turtles poster, we're impressed by her confident swagger that reeks of success.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             21. A New Element to Their Game
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:272px">
            <img alt="21. A New Element to Their Game" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/651/Pats-3_display_image_crop_272x400.jpg?1318864994" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="272"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Fans in New England expected
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/tom-brady">
             Tom Brady
            </a>
            to throw 14 touchdowns and have a 109.5 rating, but they are now pleasantly surprised that the Pats are ranked No. 6 in rushing.
           </p>
           <p>
            Whether it's from Steven Ridley or BenJarvus Green-Ellis, this team has put up 128.6 yards per game on the ground.
           </p>
           <p>
            A sexy fanbase, consistently-potent quarterback and a flourishing running game has made this team lethal.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             20. A Packed House
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:268px">
            <img alt="20. A Packed House" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/652/ph8_crop_268x400.jpg?1318864999" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="268"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Green Bay fans may still enjoy sporting the old-fashioned
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/brett-favre">
             Brett Favre
            </a>
            jerseys, but that doesn't mean they aren't thrilled about the 27-year-old Super Bowl winner who continues to tarnish opposing defenses.
           </p>
           <p>
            With 14 touchdowns (only two interceptions) and a league-best 122.9 rating,
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/aaron-rodgers">
             Aaron Rodgers
            </a>
            continues to show the league why he is perhaps the best.
           </p>
           <p>
            52 yards rushing and two touchdowns on the ground don't hurt his chances either.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             19. Kicking and Screaming
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:283px">
            <img alt="19. Kicking and Screaming" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/653/ph11_crop_283x400.jpg?1318865004" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="283"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With their No. 16 ranking on offense in yards per game and clear inability to score, the Miami Dolphins may want to focus on racking up the points through field goals.
           </p>
           <p>
            Dan Carpenter may have missed three field goals in 12 attempts this year, but his 80.2 career percentage is reminiscent of the obvious help he has in practice from enthusiastic fans.
           </p>
           <p>
            Now it's up to Matt Moore to get the ball down the field.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             16. A Black and White Legacy
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:307px">
            <img alt="16.            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After the passing of their iconic owner, Da Raidas responded with a solid win over the unimpressive Houston Texans.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/al-davis">
             Al Davis
            </a>
            (R.I.P.) instilled a culture in the Black and White that will never be forgotten.
           </p>
           <p>
            Their young core of players will continue to fight in his honor... and for their beautiful fans' appreciation.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             10. The Stinky Cheese Man
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:332px">
            <img alt="10. The Stinky Cheese Man" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/646/NFCDraft_332_crop_332x247.jpg?1318864992" height="247" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="332"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            After Aaron Rodgers threw successful chucks to 12 different receivers en route to 25 unanswered points against the Atlanta Falcons, he showed the league why he deserves the nod for best current quarterback.
           </p>
           <p>
            With fans like this cheering them on, 16-0 seems plausible.
           </p>
           <p>
            Easily the sexiest fanbase in the NFL.
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             9. Tightening Things Up
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:338px">
            <img alt="9. Tightening Things Up" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/664/Titans-1_display_image_crop_338x400.jpg?1318864998" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="338"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With nine touchdowns (only four interceptions), 1,414 yards and a 95.9 rating, Quarterback
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/matt-hasselbeck">
             Matt Hasselbeck
            </a>
            is giving Tennessee fans more hope than they expected to receive this season.
           </p>
           <p>
            If only Chris Johnson didn't seemingly decide to quit after signing his monster contract, we could see more teeth in this smile.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             8. The Missing Link
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:222px">
            <img alt="8. The Missing Link" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/665/Colts-1_crop_222x400.jpg?1318865003" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="222"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While there has been debate in the past about who should win MVP (
            <a href="http://bleacherreport.com/peyton-manning">
             Peyton Manning
            </a>
            or Tom Brady), there is no argument regarding who deserves the award this season.
           </p>
           <p>
            Tom Brady may be racking up stats on opposing defenses, but Peyton Manning is watching his team lose every week without him under center.
           </p>
           <p>
            His fans aren't pleased with the results. Manning earns is officially the Most Valuable Player.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             7. Losing at Their Own Game
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:293px">
            <img alt="7. Losing at Their Own Game" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/666/Falcons-2_crop_293x400.jpg?1318864969" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="293"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Before Week 6, the Falcons had let Seattle and Green Bay convert 15 of 26 third-down chances over those two weeks.
           </p>
           <p>
            While their defensive backfield is known as the team's main weakness, they expected their beautiful fans to create more of a distraction for opposing teams.
           </p>
           <p>
            It's only worked against them.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-46 cf display-none " data-page="46">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--prev" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Previous Page">
              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
              Prev
             </a>
             <div class="paginators_counter">

              <span class="br-light-grey">
               of
              </span>
              <span class="paginators_page-count">
               52
              </span>
             </div>
             <a class="paginator paginator--secondary paginator--next" href="javascript: void(0)" title="Next Page">

              <span class="aquo">
               
              </span>
             </a>
            </div>
            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             6. The World in His Hands
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:312px">
            <img alt="6. The World in His Hands" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/635/Redskins3_display_image_crop_312x400.jpg?1318864972" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="312"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The NFC East is for the taking, and the promising Redskins seem destined to grab it by horns and ride it to the playoffs.
           </p>
           <p>
            With fans like this supporting them, the sixth-ranked defense in yards allowed should have no problem attacking distracted opposing offenses, while Rex Grossman and his six touchdowns continues to excite skeptical analysts.
           </p>
           <p>
            Things finally seem to be turning around in Washington... so far.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-47 cf display-none " data-page="47">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             5. Practicing the Snap
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:465px">
            <img alt="5. Practicing the Snap" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/667/Giants-Fan_crop_465x311.jpg?1318864974" height="311" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="465"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Tailgating is an essential part of every football game.
           </p>
           <p>
            Drinks, food and pregame warmups... it doesn't quite get better.
           </p>
           <p>
            Especially when the beautiful fans can snap the ball.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-48 cf display-none " data-page="48">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

              <span class="aquo">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             4. The Replacements
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:278px">
            <img alt="4. The Replacements" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/633/dolphinschick_display_image_crop_278x400.jpg?1318864975" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="278"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Dolphins may be lacking excitement on the field amidst a winless season thus far, but their fanbase is holding their own in the stands.
           </p>
           <p>
            Perhaps the team should sign some distractions on to the squad in an attempt to switch things up.
           </p>
           <p>
            Tony Sparano has nothing to lose at this point.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-49 cf display-none " data-page="49">
          <header class="article_page-header">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             3. A Fan Favorite
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:308px">
            <img alt="3. A Fan Favorite" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/663/Texans-2_display_image_crop_308x400.jpg?1318864977" height="400" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="308"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            While Andre Johnson is dealing with a frustrating hamstring injury, his fans will undoubtedly feel empty knowing that the Texans lack his physicality at wide receiver without him.
           </p>
           <p>
            Matt Shaub is surely the most upset.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-50 cf display-none " data-page="50">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             2. It Ain't over Til the Sexy Fan Sings
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:281px">
            <img alt="2. It Ain't over Til the Sexy Fan Sings" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/649/nfl-jersey-girls-48_crop_281x420.jpg?1318864980" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="281"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            At least the cameras had something worth looking at during the Chiefs' 0-3 start to the season.
           </p>
           <p>
            However, after two consecutive wins, a bye week and two huge division games against the Oakland Raiders and San Diego Chargers, Kansas City isn't going down without a fight.
           </p>
           <p>
            Neither are their fans.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-51 cf display-none " data-page="51">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             1. Make or Break
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:590px">
            <img alt="1. Make or Break" data-defer-src="http://cdn.bleacherreport.net/images_root/slides/photos/001/427/636/giants-sexy-f_crop_590x300.jpg?1318864979" height="300" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="590"/>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            With two interceptions in four games, Eli Manning was finally settling down like his loyal fans... until he threw a crucial mistake on the final drive of last week's debacle against the Seahawks.
           </p>
           <p>
            A huge 27-24 win over the feisty Buffalo Bills made fans forget.
           </p>
           <p>
            This fan seemed ready to cover her eyes.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

        // If we've already installed the SDK, we're done
        if (document.getElementById('facebook-jssdk')) {return;}

        // Get the first script element, which we'll use to find the parent node
